\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00380}00380 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Return pointer to greater or equal-\/sized edge neighbour}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00381}00381 \textcolor{comment}{  /// in specified \(\backslash\)c direction; also provide info regarding the relative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00382}00382 \textcolor{comment}{  /// size and orientation of neighbour:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00383}00383 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ The vector translate\_s turns the index of the local coordinate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00384}00384 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   in the present quadtree into that of the neighbour. If there are no}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00385}00385 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   rotations then translate\_s[i] = i, but if, for example, the neighbour's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00386}00386 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   eastern face is adjacent to our northern face translate\_s[0] = 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00387}00387 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   and translate\_s[1] = 0. Of course, this could be deduced after the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00388}00388 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   fact, but it's easier to do it here.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00389}00389 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ Let's have a look at the current quadtree's edge in the specified}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00390}00390 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   direction. The edge will be parallel to one of the two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00391}00391 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   local coordinates in the element. This edge has two}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00392}00392 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   vertices. The vertex at the minimum value of the local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00393}00393 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   coordinate (the "{}lo"{} vertex) is located}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00394}00394 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   at the local coordinates (\(\backslash\)c s\_lo[0], \(\backslash\)c s\_lo[1]) in the neighbouring}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00395}00395 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   quadtree.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00396}00396 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ ditto with s\_hi: The vertex at the maximum value of the local}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00397}00397 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   coordinate located at the local coordinates (\(\backslash\)c s\_hi[0],}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00398}00398 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   \(\backslash\)c s\_hi[1]) in the neighbouring quadtree.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00399}00399 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ We're looking for a neighbour in the specified \(\backslash\)c direction. When}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00400}00400 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   viewed from the neighbouring quadtree, the edge that separates}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00401}00401 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   the present quadtree from its neighbour is the neighbour's \(\backslash\)c edge}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00402}00402 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   edge. If there's no rotation between the two quadtrees, this is a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00403}00403 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   simple reflection: For instance, if we're looking}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00404}00404 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   for a neighhbour in the \(\backslash\)c N [orthern] \(\backslash\)c direction, \(\backslash\)c edge will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00405}00405 \textcolor{comment}{  ///   be \(\backslash\)c S [outh]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{quadtree_8cc_source_l00406}00406 \textcolor{comment}{  /// -\/ \(\backslash\)c diff\_level <= 0 indicates the difference in refinement levels between}}
